### [115] [Lumbermark: Resistant Clustering by Chopping Up Mutual Reachability Minimum Spanning Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07143)
*Marek Gagolewski*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Lumbermark是一种鲁棒的分裂聚类算法，能够检测不同大小、密度和形状的簇，通过互达距离最小生成树的切割实现聚类，可作为HDBSCAN的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有聚类算法在处理不同大小、密度和形状的簇时存在局限性，需要一种更鲁棒的算法来应对复杂的数据分布，特别是能够平滑数据分布并减少低密度对象影响的算法。

Method: Lumbermark使用互达距离构建最小生成树，通过迭代切割树中突出的连接段来分离簇。互达距离平滑了数据分布并减少了噪声点和离群值的影响，算法可视为HDBSCAN的替代方案，能够生成用户指定大小的分区。

Result: 算法在基准数据上表现良好，提供了Python和R的开源实现包'lumbermark'，该实现快速且易于使用。

Conclusion: Lumbermark是一种有效的聚类算法，能够处理复杂的数据结构，有望成为数据科学家和从业者的有用工具。

Abstract: We introduce Lumbermark, a robust divisive clustering algorithm capable of detecting clusters of varying sizes, densities, and shapes. Lumbermark iteratively chops off large limbs connected by protruding segments of a dataset's mutual reachability minimum spanning tree. The use of mutual reachability distances smoothens the data distribution and decreases the influence of low-density objects, such as noise points between clusters or outliers at their peripheries. The algorithm can be viewed as an alternative to HDBSCAN that produces partitions with user-specified sizes. A fast, easy-to-use implementation of the new method is available in the open-source 'lumbermark' package for Python and R. We show that Lumbermark performs well on benchmark data and hope it will prove useful to data scientists and practitioners across different fields.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 情感标注本质上是主观且认知要求高的任务，会产生反映不同标注者感知差异的信号。传统方法将这种变异性压缩为均值或中位数等点估计，丢弃了标注者分歧和不确定性的宝贵信息。

Method: 提出分布感知框架，使用Beta分布建模标注共识。模型预测标注分布的均值和标准差，通过矩匹配转换为有效的Beta参数。这种公式化能够以闭式形式恢复高阶分布描述符，包括偏度、峰度和分位数。

Result: 在SEWA和RECOLA数据集上使用多模态特征进行评估。实验结果表明，基于Beta的建模产生的预测分布与经验标注分布紧密匹配，同时在与传统回归方法的比较中表现出竞争力。

Abstract: Emotion annotation is inherently subjective and cognitively demanding, producing signals that reflect diverse perceptions across annotators rather than a single ground truth. In continuous affect prediction, this variability is typically collapsed into point estimates such as the mean or median, discarding valuable information about annotator disagreement and uncertainty. In this work, we propose a distribution-aware framework that models annotation consensus using the Beta distribution. Instead of predicting a single affect value, models estimate the mean and standard deviation of the annotation distribution, which are transformed into valid Beta parameters through moment matching. This formulation enables the recovery of higher-order distributional descriptors, including skewness, kurtosis, and quantiles, in closed form. As a result, the model captures not only the central tendency of emotional perception but also variability, asymmetry, and uncertainty in annotator responses. We evaluate the proposed approach on the SEWA and RECOLA datasets using multimodal features. Experimental results show that Beta-based modelling produces predictive distributions that closely match the empirical annotator distributions while achieving competitive performance with conventional regression approaches. These findings highlight the importance of modelling annotation uncertainty in affective computing and demonstrate the potential of distribution-aware learning for subjective signal analysis.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维数据通常位于低维流形附近，但现有方法需要显式的几何结构（如坐标图、投影等）。本文旨在仅使用点云样本，在不需要几何原语的情况下，在底层流形上构建扩散过程。

Method: 基于数据构建邻近图，从图中估计扩散过程的无穷小生成器及其carré-du-champ（CDC），这两者共同编码了目标扩散的局部随机和几何结构。提出了隐式流形值扩散（IMDs）构造，并使用欧拉-丸山积分进行数值模拟。

Result: 证明了随着样本数量的增加，诱导过程在概率路径空间上依分布收敛到其光滑流形对应物。这为数据流形上的扩散动力学提供了严格的实践基础。

Abstract: High-dimensional data are often modeled as lying near a low-dimensional manifold. We study how to construct diffusion processes on this data manifold in the implicit setting. That is, using only point cloud samples and without access to charts, projections, or other geometric primitives. Our main contribution is a data-driven SDE that captures intrinsic diffusion on the underlying manifold while being defined in ambient space. The construction relies on estimating the diffusion's infinitesimal generator and its carré-du-champ (CDC) from a proximity graph built from the data. The generator and CDC together encode the local stochastic and geometric structure of the intended diffusion. We show that, as the number of samples grows, the induced process converges in law on the space of probability paths to its smooth manifold counterpart. We call this construction Implicit Manifold-valued Diffusions (IMDs), and furthermore present a numerical simulation procedure using Euler-Maruyama integration. This gives a rigorous basis for practical implementations of diffusion dynamics on data manifolds, and opens new directions for manifold-aware sampling, exploration, and generative modeling.

### [120] [How Does Machine Learning Manage Complexity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07233)
*Lance Fortnow*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文通过计算复杂性视角分析机器学习模型的能力，特别是它们建模复杂系统的能力，关注可计算分布而非更广泛的样本分布，并展示了如果模型能最小化与密码学伪随机生成器分布误差，则其分布必须接近均匀分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在通过计算复杂性理论来理解机器学习模型的能力边界，特别是它们如何建模复杂系统。传统机器学习通常处理从可采样或更复杂分布中抽取的数据，但作者认为通过专注于可计算分布，机器学习模型能更好地通过概率管理复杂性。

Method: 作者将机器学习抽象为产生具有多项式有界最大熵的P/poly可计算分布的过程，而不关注具体学习机制。通过理论分析，展示了如果机器学习模型产生的分布μ能最小化与密码学伪随机生成器生成分布的误差，则μ必须接近均匀分布。

Result: 主要理论结果是：如果机器学习模型产生的分布μ能够最小化与密码学伪随机生成器生成分布的误差，那么μ必须接近均匀分布。这说明了机器学习模型在建模某些复杂分布时的固有局限性。

Conclusion: 通过计算复杂性视角分析机器学习模型，揭示了它们在建模复杂系统时的能力边界。专注于可计算分布有助于更好地管理复杂性，但某些密码学强分布（如伪随机生成器产生的分布）对机器学习模型提出了根本性挑战，导致模型只能产生接近均匀的分布。

Abstract: We provide a computational complexity lens to understand the power of machine learning models, particularly their ability to model complex systems.
  Machine learning models are often trained on data drawn from sampleable or more complex distributions, a far wider range of distributions than just computable ones. By focusing on computable distributions, machine learning models can better manage complexity via probability. We abstract away from specific learning mechanisms, modeling machine learning as producing P/poly-computable distributions with polynomially-bounded max-entropy.
  We illustrate how learning computable distributions models complexity by showing that if a machine learning model produces a distribution $μ$ that minimizes error against the distribution generated by a cryptographic pseudorandom generator, then $μ$ must be close to uniform.

### [121] [On the Price of Privacy for Language Identification and Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07238)
*Xiaoyu Li,Andi Han,Jiaojiao Jiang,Junbin Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了语言模型在差分隐私下的语言识别和生成任务，发现近似差分隐私下可达到与非隐私相同的错误率，而纯差分隐私下错误率指数会降低min{1,ε}倍，且这一界限是紧的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型越来越多地在敏感用户数据上训练，理解语言学习中隐私的基本成本变得至关重要。研究在不可知统计设置下的差分隐私语言识别和生成任务，建立算法并匹配下界以精确量化隐私成本。

Method: 在不可知统计设置下研究差分隐私语言识别和生成任务，建立算法并推导匹配的下界。分析近似(ε,δ)-DP和纯ε-DP两种隐私设置下的性能界限。

Result: 对于近似(ε,δ)-DP（常数ε>0），语言识别和生成都能恢复非隐私错误率：识别为exp(-r(n))（任意r(n)=o(n)），生成为exp(-Ω(n))。对于纯ε-DP，指数会降低min{1,ε}倍，且这一界限是紧的。对于生成任务，在温和假设下，上界exp(-min{1,ε}·Ω(n))与下界匹配（相差常数倍），建立了最优速率。

Conclusion: 语言学习中的隐私成本出人意料地温和：在近似差分隐私下完全不存在，在纯差分隐私下仅为指数中的min{1,ε}因子。这表明隐私保护在语言学习任务中可以实现而不显著牺牲性能。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly trained on sensitive user data, understanding the fundamental cost of privacy in language learning becomes essential. We initiate the study of differentially private (DP) language identification and generation in the agnostic statistical setting, establishing algorithms and matching lower bounds that precisely quantify the cost of privacy. For both tasks, approximate $(\varepsilon, δ)$-DP with constant $\varepsilon > 0$ recovers the non-private error rates: $\exp(-r(n))$ for identification (for any $r(n) = o(n)$) and $\exp(-Ω(n))$ for generation. Under pure $\varepsilon$-DP, the exponents degrade by a multiplicative factor of $\min\{1, \varepsilon\}$, which we show is tight up to constants. Notably, for generation under pure DP with mild assumptions, the upper bound $\exp(-\min\{1,\varepsilon\} \cdot Ω(n))$ matches the lower bound up to some constants, establishing an optimal rate. Our results show that the cost of privacy in language learning is surprisingly mild: absent entirely under approximate DP, and exactly a $\min\{1,\varepsilon\}$ factor in the exponent under pure DP.

### [125] [Android Coach: Improve Online Agentic Training Efficiency with Single State Multiple Actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07277)
*Guo Gan,Yuxuan Ding,Cong Chen,Yuwei Ren,Yin Huang,Hong Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Android Coach是一个新的在线强化学习框架，通过从单个在线状态采样多个动作（单状态多动作范式）来提升Android智能体的训练效率，避免了模拟器的高延迟成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前在线强化学习方法在Android智能体训练中存在效率低下的问题，主要原因是模拟器高延迟和现有RL算法的样本效率低。现有方法采用单状态单动作范式，每个昂贵的模拟器状态只更新一次策略，未能充分利用每个状态。

Method: 提出Android Coach框架，将训练范式从单状态单动作转变为单状态多动作，允许智能体从单个在线状态采样多个动作。通过训练一个评估动作价值的critic来实现，无需额外模拟器开销。为确保critic的可靠性，集成了过程奖励模型并引入了基于平均critic输出的组间优势估计器。

Result: 在AndroidLab和AndroidWorld上分别实现了7.5%和8.3%的成功率提升（相比UI-TARS-1.5-7B）。在相同成功率下，训练效率比PPO和GRPO等单状态单动作方法提高了1.4倍。

Conclusion: Android Coach通过单状态多动作范式有效解决了Android智能体在线强化学习中的效率问题，显著提升了训练效率和成功率，为移动应用自动化任务提供了更高效的训练框架。

Abstract: Online reinforcement learning (RL) serves as an effective method for enhancing the capabilities of Android agents. However, guiding agents to learn through online interaction is prohibitively expensive due to the high latency of emulators and the sample inefficiency of existing RL algorithms. We identify a fundamental limitation in current approaches: the Single State Single Action paradigm, which updates the policy with one-to-one state-action pairs from online one-way rollouts without fully exploring each costly emulator state. In this paper, we propose Android Coach, a novel framework that shifts the training paradigm to Single State Multiple Actions, allowing the agent to sample and utilize multiple actions for a single online state. We enable this without additional emulator overhead by learning a critic that estimates action values. To ensure the critic serves as a reliable coach, we integrate a process reward model and introduce a group-wise advantage estimator based on the averaged critic outputs. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness and efficiency of Android Coach: it achieves 7.5% and 8.3% success rate improvements on AndroidLab and AndroidWorld over UI-TARS-1.5-7B, and attains 1.4x higher training efficiency than Single State Single Action methods PPO and GRPO at matched success rates.

*Sam Gunn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种数据删除方案，能够在深度学习设置中预测模型输出，误差趋近于零，计算和存储复杂度仅为多项式级别


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究训练数据选择如何影响AI模型，这是可解释性、隐私和基础科学的核心问题，核心是数据删除问题：在合理预计算后，快速预测如果某个训练数据子集被排除在学习算法之外，模型在给定情况下的行为

Method: 基于"稳定性"假设的数据删除方案，使用新的局部草图技术，通过在随机复数方向上计算高阶导数来局部草图化算术电路，利用前向模式自动微分廉价计算这些导数

Result: 提出的数据删除方案能够以趋近于零的误差预测模型输出，预计算和预测算法仅比常规训练和推理慢多项式因子，存储需求仅为多项式数量的模型

Conclusion: 该方法基于稳定性假设，与学习强大AI模型完全兼容，在microgpt的最小实验集中得到验证，为数据删除问题提供了高效解决方案

Abstract: How does the choice of training data influence an AI model? This question is of central importance to interpretability, privacy, and basic science. At its core is the data deletion problem: after a reasonable amount of precomputation, quickly predict how the model would behave in a given situation if a given subset of training data had been excluded from the learning algorithm.
  We present a data deletion scheme capable of predicting model outputs with vanishing error $\varepsilon$ in the deep learning setting. Our precomputation and prediction algorithms are only $\mathrm{poly}(1/\varepsilon)$ factors slower than regular training and inference, respectively. The storage requirements are those of $\mathrm{poly}(1/\varepsilon)$ models.
  Our proof is based on an assumption that we call "stability." In contrast to the assumptions made by prior work, stability appears to be fully compatible with learning powerful AI models. In support of this, we show that stability is satisfied in a minimal set of experiments with microgpt. Our code is available at https://github.com/SamSpo1/microgpt-sketch.
  At a technical level, our work is based on a new method for locally sketching an arithmetic circuit by computing higher-order derivatives in random complex directions. Forward-mode automatic differentiation allows cheap computation of these derivatives.

</details>

### [127] [Occlusion Handling by Pushing for Enhanced Fruit Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06341)
*Ege Gursoy,Dana Kulić,Andrea Cherubini*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种农业机器人系统，通过推开遮挡果实的树枝来提高果实可见性，结合深度学习、传统图像处理和3D霍夫变换技术


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在农业机器人中，果实被树枝和树叶遮挡会导致错误的果实定位或阻碍机器人采摘。需要一种方法来推开遮挡果实的树枝以提高可见性

Method: 使用RGB-D相机和机械臂，首先在RGB图像中检测被遮挡的果实，通过深度学习生成模型在深度空间估计被遮挡部分；使用传统图像处理技术确定推开方向；引入3D霍夫变换检测点云中的直线段以识别遮挡树枝；最后用机械臂推开树枝

Result: 在不同光照条件和多种水果（苹果、柠檬、橙子）的真实数据上验证了感知方法，实现了可见性改善和成功的遮挡清除，并通过真实机器人树枝推开演示展示了实际应用

Conclusion: 该方法成功结合了深度学习、传统图像处理和3D霍夫变换，有效解决了农业机器人中果实被遮挡的问题，提高了果实可见性和采摘成功率

Abstract: In agricultural robotics, effective observation and localization of fruits present challenges due to occlusions caused by other parts of the tree, such as branches and leaves. These occlusions can result in false fruit localization or impede the robot from picking the fruit. The objective of this work is to push away branches that block the fruit's view to increase their visibility. Our setup consists of an RGB-D camera and a robot arm. First, we detect the occluded fruit in the RGB image and estimate its occluded part via a deep learning generative model in the depth space. The direction to push to clear the occlusions is determined using classic image processing techniques. We then introduce a 3D extension of the 2D Hough transform to detect straight line segments in the point cloud. This extension helps detect tree branches and identify the one mainly responsible for the occlusion. Finally, we clear the occlusion by pushing the branch with the robot arm. Our method uses a combination of deep learning for fruit appearance estimation, classic image processing for push direction determination, and 3D Hough transform for branch detection. We validate our perception methods through real data under different lighting conditions and various types of fruits (i.e. apple, lemon, orange), achieving improved visibility and successful occlusion clearance. We demonstrate the practical application of our approach through a real robot branch pushing demonstration.

</details>

*Xuying Huang,Sicong Pan,Delphine Reinhardt,Maren Bennewitz*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现用户偏好隐私保护视觉抽象和捕获时低分辨率保护机制；偏好的RGB分辨率取决于期望的隐私级别和机器人导航时的接近程度。

Existing approaches to privacy-preserving navigation-oriented visual perception have largely been driven by technical considerations, with limited grounding in user privacy preferences. In this work, we propose a user-centered approach to designing privacy-preserving visual perception for robot navigation. To investigate how user privacy preferences can inform such design, we conducted two user studies. The results show that users prefer privacy-preserving visual abstractions and capture-time low-resolution preservation mechanisms: their preferred RGB resolution depends both on the desired privacy level and robot proximity during navigation. Based on these findings, we further derive a user-configurable distance-to-resolution privacy policy for privacy-preserving robot visual navigation.

### [129] [Uncertainty Estimation for Deep Reconstruction in Actuatic Disaster Scenarios with Autonomous Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06387)

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 比较四种方法在稀疏观测下环境标量场重建与不确定性分解的性能，发现证据深度学习在精度、校准和推理成本上表现最佳

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主水下车辆进行环境监测时，需要从稀疏观测中准确重建标量场，同时进行可靠的不确定性量化以支持主动感知策略

Method: 比较了四种方法：高斯过程、蒙特卡洛Dropout、深度集成学习和证据深度学习，在三种代表性传感器感知模型下进行标量场重建和不确定性分解

Result: 证据深度学习在所有传感器配置下实现了最佳的重建精度和不确定性校准，且推理成本最低；高斯过程受限于平稳核假设，在观测密度增加时变得不可行

Abstract: Accurate reconstruction of environmental scalar fields from sparse onboard observations is essential for autonomous vehicles engaged in aquatic monitoring. Beyond point estimates, principled uncertainty quantification is critical for active sensing strategies such as Informative Path Planning, where epistemic uncertainty drives data collection decisions. This paper compares Gaussian Processes, Monte Carlo Dropout, Deep Ensembles, and Evidential Deep Learning for simultaneous scalar field reconstruction and uncertainty decomposition under three perceptual models representative of real sensor modalities. Results show that Evidential Deep Learning achieves the best reconstruction accuracy and uncertainty calibration across all sensor configurations at the lowest inference cost, while Gaussian Processes are fundamentally limited by their stationary kernel assumption and become intractable as observation density grows. These findings support Evidential Deep Learning as the preferred method for uncertainty-aware field reconstruction in real-time autonomous vehicle deployments.

For dataset, we propose a novel bimanual grasp synthesis pipeline to efficiently annotate physically feasible data for dataset construction. This pipeline addresses the challenges of high-dimensional bimanual grasping through a two-stage synthesis strategy of efficient region-based grasp initialization and decoupled force-closure grasp optimization. Powered by this pipeline, we construct a large-scale bimanual dexterous grasp dataset, comprising 6351 diverse objects with sizes ranging from 30 to 80 cm, along with 9.7 million annotated grasp data. Based on this dataset, we further introduce a bimanual-coordinated and geometry-size-adaptive dexterous grasping generation framework. The framework lies in two key designs: a bimanual coordination module and a geometry-size-adaptive grasp generation strategy to generate coordinated and high-quality grasps on unseen objects. Extensive experiments conducted in both simulation and real world demonstrate the superior performance of our proposed data synthesis pipeline and learned generative framework.

### [131] [Train-Small Deploy-Large: Leveraging Diffusion-Based Multi-Robot Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06598)
*Siddharth Singh,Soumee Guha,Qing Chang,Scott Acton*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出基于扩散模型的多机器人路径规划方法，能够处理动态变化的机器人数量，实现"小训练大部署"范式


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于学习的多机器人路径规划方法难以扩展到变化的机器人数量，特别是部署时机器人数量增加的情况。大多数方法在固定数量机器人上训练，测试时可能容忍数量减少，但数量增加时通常失败。同时，为更多智能体训练这些方法既耗时又计算昂贵。而分析方法在计算扩展性或处理环境动态变化方面存在困难。

Method: 提出基于扩散模型的规划器，能够处理动态变化的智能体数量。方法采用单个共享的扩散模型规划器，结合专用的智能体间注意力计算和时间卷积。在有限数量的智能体上进行训练，但在部署时能有效泛化到更多智能体。

Result: 结果显示，集成单个共享扩散模型规划器与专用智能体间注意力计算和时间卷积，能够实现"小训练大部署"范式，并保持良好准确性。在多种场景中验证了方法，并与现有多智能体强化学习技术和启发式控制方法进行了性能比较。

Conclusion: 提出的基于扩散模型的多机器人路径规划方法能够有效处理动态变化的智能体数量，实现从少量训练智能体到大量部署智能体的泛化，为解决多机器人路径规划中的可扩展性和泛化问题提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Learning based multi-robot path planning methods struggle to scale or generalize to changes, particularly variations in the number of robots during deployment. Most existing methods are trained on a fixed number of robots and may tolerate a reduced number during testing, but typically fail when the number increases. Additionally, training such methods for a larger number of agents can be both time consuming and computationally expensive. However, analytical methods can struggle to scale computationally or handle dynamic changes in the environment. In this work, we propose to leverage a diffusion model based planner capable of handling dynamically varying number of agents. Our approach is trained on a limited number of agents and generalizes effectively to larger numbers of agents during deployment. Results show that integrating a single shared diffusion model based planner with dedicated inter-agent attention computation and temporal convolution enables a train small deploy-large paradigm with good accuracy. We validate our method across multiple scenarios and compare the performance with existing multi-agent reinforcement learning techniques and heuristic control based methods.

### [132] [RichMap: A Reachability Map Balancing Precision, Efficiency, and Flexibility for Rich Robot Manipulation Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06778)
*Yupu Lu,Yuxiang Ma,Jia Pan*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: RichMap是一种高精度可达性地图表示方法，通过改进经典网格结构，在保持结构灵活性的同时达到接近紧凑地图形式的性能，适用于机器人操作任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在机器人操作任务中平衡效率与灵活性，需要一种既能保持高精度又能快速查询的可达性地图表示方法。传统网格结构存在效率问题，而紧凑地图形式又缺乏灵活性。

Method: 通过改进经典网格结构，利用S²（或SO(3)）的理论容量边界确保严格覆盖，采用异步流水线进行高效构建，并扩展框架应用包括最大均值差异度量工作空间相似性和基于能量的扩散策略转移指导。

Result: 验证显示高预测准确率（>98%）、低误报率（1-2%）、快速大批量查询（约15μs/查询）。在跨具身场景的方块推动实验中，通过基于能量的扩散策略转移实现了高达26%的性能提升。

Conclusion: RichMap提供了一种平衡效率与灵活性的高精度可达性地图表示方法，能够支持多种机器人操作任务，并在跨具身场景中显著提升性能。

Abstract: This paper presents RichMap, a high-precision reachability map representation designed to balance efficiency and flexibility for versatile robot manipulation tasks. By refining the classic grid-based structure, we propose a streamlined approach that achieves performance close to compact map forms (e.g., RM4D) while maintaining structural flexibility. Our method utilizes theoretical capacity bounds on $\mathbb{S}^2$ (or $SO(3)$) to ensure rigorous coverage and employs an asynchronous pipeline for efficient construction. We validate the map against comprehensive metrics, pursuing high prediction accuracy ($>98\%$), low false positive rates ($1\sim2\%$), and fast large-batch query ($\sim$15 $μ$s/query). We extend the framework applications to quantify robot workspace similarity via maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) metrics and demonstrate energy-based guidance for diffusion policy transfer, achieving up to $26\%$ improvement for cross-embodiment scenarios in the block pushing experiment.

</details>

Results indicate that zero-shot transfer leads to lower success rates and relatively longer task execution times, while fine-tuning significantly improves performance with fewer training time-steps. ### [136] [Differentiable Environment-Trajectory Co-Optimization for Safe Multi-Agent Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06972)
*Zhan Gao,Gabriele Fadini,Stelian Coros,Amanda Prorok*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种双层优化框架，将环境配置作为决策变量与智能体动作联合优化，以实现安全导航。通过可微分优化方法迭代求解智能体轨迹和环境配置，利用KKT条件和隐函数定理计算梯度，并提出了量化导航安全性的新度量指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多智能体导航方法将环境视为固定不变，忽略了环境配置对智能体性能的影响。本文认为环境配置应与智能体动作共同优化，以在空间约束、规则和限制下实现更安全的导航。

Method: 提出双层优化问题：下层子问题优化智能体轨迹以最小化导航成本，上层子问题优化环境配置以最大化导航安全性。开发可微分优化方法，使用内点法求解下层问题，梯度上升法求解上层问题。利用KKT条件和隐函数定理计算智能体轨迹对环境参数的梯度，实现双层结构的可微分性。提出量化导航安全性的新度量指标。

Result: 实验在从仓库物流到城市交通等多种安全关键导航场景中验证了框架的有效性。结果表明，优化后的环境能够提供导航指导，同时提高智能体的安全性和效率。

Conclusion: 将环境配置作为决策变量与智能体动作联合优化的方法能够显著改善多智能体导航的安全性和效率，为安全关键导航场景提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: The environment plays a critical role in multi-agent navigation by imposing spatial constraints, rules, and limitations that agents must navigate around. Traditional approaches treat the environment as fixed, without exploring its impact on agents' performance. This work considers environment configurations as decision variables, alongside agent actions, to jointly achieve safe navigation. We formulate a bi-level problem, where the lower-level sub-problem optimizes agent trajectories that minimize navigation cost and the upper-level sub-problem optimizes environment configurations that maximize navigation safety. We develop a differentiable optimization method that iteratively solves the lower-level sub-problem with interior point methods and the upper-level sub-problem with gradient ascent. A key challenge lies in analytically coupling these two levels. We address this by leveraging KKT conditions and the Implicit Function Theorem to compute gradients of agent trajectories w.r.t. environment parameters, enabling differentiation throughout the bi-level structure. Moreover, we propose a novel metric that quantifies navigation safety as a criterion for the upper-level environment optimization, and prove its validity through measure theory. Our experiments validate the effectiveness of the proposed framework in a variety of safety-critical navigation scenarios, inspired from warehouse logistics to urban transportation. The results demonstrate that optimized environments provide navigation guidance, improving both agents' safety and efficiency.

### [137] [KITE: Keyframe-Indexed Tokenized Evidence for VLM-Based Robot Failure Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07034)
*Mehdi Hosseinzadeh,King Hang Wong,Feras Dayoub*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: KITE是一个无需训练、基于关键帧锚定、布局接地的前端系统，将长机器人执行视频转换为紧凑、可解释的标记化证据，供视觉语言模型使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要将长机器人执行视频转换为紧凑、可解释的表示形式，以便视觉语言模型能够进行机器人故障分析（检测、识别、定位、解释和纠正）。

Method: KITE将每个轨迹提炼为一小组运动显著的关键帧，包含开放词汇检测，并将每个关键帧与示意性鸟瞰图表示配对，编码相对对象布局、轴、时间戳和检测置信度。这些视觉线索与机器人配置和场景上下文标记序列化为统一提示。

Result: 在RoboFAC基准测试中，KITE与Qwen2.5-VL组合在无需训练设置下显著优于原始Qwen2.5-VL，在模拟故障检测、识别和定位方面有特别大的提升，同时与RoboFAC调优基线保持竞争力。小型QLoRA微调进一步提高了解释和纠正质量。

Conclusion: KITE作为结构化、可解释的前端系统，能够有效支持机器人故障分析，在真实双臂机器人上展示了实际应用价值，为机器人故障分析提供了实用的解决方案。

Abstract: We present KITE, a training-free, keyframe-anchored, layout-grounded front-end that converts long robot-execution videos into compact, interpretable tokenized evidence for vision-language models (VLMs). KITE distills each trajectory into a small set of motion-salient keyframes with open-vocabulary detections and pairs each keyframe with a schematic bird's-eye-view (BEV) representation that encodes relative object layout, axes, timestamps, and detection confidence. These visual cues are serialized with robot-profile and scene-context tokens into a unified prompt, allowing the same front-end to support failure detection, identification, localization, explanation, and correction with an off-the-shelf VLM. On the RoboFAC benchmark, KITE with Qwen2.5-VL substantially improves over vanilla Qwen2.5-VL in the training-free setting, with especially large gains on simulation failure detection, identification, and localization, while remaining competitive with a RoboFAC-tuned baseline. A small QLoRA fine-tune further improves explanation and correction quality. We also report qualitative results on real dual-arm robots, demonstrating the practical applicability of KITE as a structured and interpretable front-end for robot failure analysis. Code and models are released on our project page: https://m80hz.github.io/kite/

### [138] [AEROS: A Single-Agent Operating Architecture with Embodied Capability Modules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07039)
*Xue Qin,Simin Luan,Cong Yang,Zhijun Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人系统缺乏统一原则来组织智能、能力和执行，要么采用耦合的单体架构，要么分解为松散协调的模块或多智能体，缺乏一致的身份和控制权限模型。

Method: 提出AEROS框架，将每个机器人建模为单一持久智能体，通过具身能力模块提供功能，ECM封装可执行技能、模型和工具，执行约束和安全保证由策略分离的运行时强制执行。

Result: 在PyBullet仿真中，Franka Panda机械臂的8个实验显示：AEROS在三个任务中达到100%成功率（基线为67-93%），策略层完全阻止无效动作，运行时优势跨任务泛化，ECM运行时加载后100%成功。

Abstract: Robotic systems lack a principled abstraction for organizing intelligence, capabilities, and execution in a unified manner. Existing approaches either couple skills within monolithic architectures or decompose functionality into loosely coordinated modules or multiple agents, often without a coherent model of identity and control authority. We argue that a robot should be modeled as a single persistent intelligent subject whose capabilities are extended through installable packages. We formalize this view as AEROS (Agent Execution Runtime Operating System), in which each robot corresponds to one persistent agent and capabilities are provided through Embodied Capability Modules (ECMs). Each ECM encapsulates executable skills, models, and tools, while execution constraints and safety guarantees are enforced by a policy-separated runtime. This separation enables modular extensibility, composable capability execution, and consistent system-level safety. We evaluate a reference implementation in PyBullet simulation with a Franka Panda 7-DOF manipulator across eight experiments covering re-planning, failure recovery, policy enforcement, baseline comparison, cross-task generality, ECM hot-swapping, ablation, and failure boundary analysis. Over 100 randomized trials per condition, AEROS achieves 100% task success across three tasks versus baselines (BehaviorTree.CPP-style and ProgPrompt-style at 92--93%, flat pipeline at 67--73%), the policy layer blocks all invalid actions with zero false acceptances, runtime benefits generalize across tasks without task-specific tuning, and ECMs load at runtime with 100% post-swap success.

*Davood Soleymanzadeh,Xiao Liang,Minghui Zheng*

TL;DR: Flow Motion Policy是一种用于机器人机械臂的端到端神经运动规划器，利用流匹配方法生成多条可行路径，通过推理时优化提高规划成功率


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开环端到端神经运动规划器通常只生成单一路径，且未充分利用其开环结构进行推理时优化，无法处理规划数据集固有的多模态特性

Method: 采用流匹配方法的随机生成框架，对可行路径分布进行建模，支持推理时最佳N采样，生成多条端到端候选路径，规划后评估碰撞状态并执行首个无碰撞解

Result: 相比代表性采样基和神经运动规划方法，Flow Motion Policy提高了规划成功率和效率，证明了随机生成策略在端到端运动规划和推理时优化中的有效性

Conclusion: 流匹配的随机生成框架能有效捕捉规划数据集的多模态特性，通过推理时优化显著提升机器人机械臂运动规划性能

Abstract: Open-loop end-to-end neural motion planners have recently been proposed to improve motion planning for robotic manipulators. These methods enable planning directly from sensor observations without relying on a privileged collision checker during planning. However, many existing methods generate only a single path for a given workspace across different runs, and do not leverage their open-loop structure for inference-time optimization. To address this limitation, we introduce Flow Motion Policy, an open-loop, end-to-end neural motion planner for robotic manipulators that leverages the stochastic generative formulation of flow matching methods to capture the inherent multi-modality of planning datasets. By modeling a distribution over feasible paths, Flow Motion Policy enables efficient inference-time best-of-$N$ sampling. The method generates multiple end-to-end candidate paths, evaluates their collision status after planning, and executes the first collision-free solution. We benchmark the Flow Motion Policy against representative sampling-based and neural motion planning methods. Evaluation results demonstrate that Flow Motion Policy improves planning success and efficiency, highlighting the effectiveness of stochastic generative policies for end-to-end motion planning and inference-time optimization. Experimental evaluation videos are available via this \href{https://zh.engr.tamu.edu/wp-content/uploads/sites/310/2026/03/FMP-Website.mp4}{link}.

### [141] [An RTK-SLAM Dataset for Absolute Accuracy Evaluation in GNSS-Degraded Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07151)
*Wei Zhang,Vincent Ress,David Skuddis,Uwe Soergel,Norbert Haala*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: RTK-SLAM系统评估中常用的SE(3)对齐方法会掩盖全局误差，本文提出了新的数据集和评估方法，分离RTK输入和地面真值，揭示SE(3)对齐可能低估76%的绝对定位误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RTK-SLAM评估方法使用SE(3)对齐来评估轨迹误差，这种方法会吸收全局漂移和系统误差，导致评估结果过于乐观，无法准确反映RTK-SLAM的全局精度。需要新的数据集和评估方法来暴露这一缺陷。

Method: 提出了新的地理参考数据集和评估方法，关键设计原则是将RTK接收器仅作为系统输入，而地面真值通过大地测量全站仪独立建立。数据集包含两个场景，使用手持RTK-SLAM设备采集，评估了LiDAR-惯性、视觉-惯性和LiDAR-视觉-惯性RTK-SLAM系统。

Result: SE(3)对齐可能低估高达76%的绝对定位误差。RTK-SLAM在开阔天空条件下能达到厘米级绝对精度，在室内环境下保持分米级全局精度，而独立RTK在室内会退化到数十米误差。

Conclusion: 需要新的评估标准来准确评估RTK-SLAM的全局精度，提出的数据集和方法能够暴露SE(3)对齐的局限性，为RTK-SLAM系统提供更真实的性能评估。

Abstract: RTK-SLAM systems integrate simultaneous localization and mapping (SLAM) with real-time kinematic (RTK) GNSS positioning, promising both relative consistency and globally referenced coordinates for efficient georeferenced surveying. A critical and underappreciated issue is that the standard evaluation metric, Absolute Trajectory Error (ATE), first fits an optimal rigid-body transformation between the estimated trajectory and reference before computing errors. This so-called SE(3) alignment absorbs global drift and systematic errors, making trajectories appear more accurate than they are in practice, and is unsuitable for evaluating the global accuracy of RTK-SLAM. We present a geodetically referenced dataset and evaluation methodology that expose this gap. A key design principle is that the RTK receiver is used solely as a system input, while ground truth is established independently via a geodetic total station. This separation is absent from all existing datasets, where GNSS typically serves as (part of) the ground truth. The dataset is collected with a handheld RTK-SLAM device, comprising two scenes. We evaluate LiDAR-inertial, visual-inertial, and LiDAR-visual-inertial RTK-SLAM systems alongside standalone RTK, reporting direct global accuracy and SE(3)-aligned relative accuracy to make the gap explicit. Results show that SE(3) alignment can underestimate absolute positioning error by up to 76\%. RTK-SLAM achieves centimeter-level absolute accuracy in open-sky conditions and maintains decimeter-level global accuracy indoors, where standalone RTK degrades to tens of meters. The dataset, calibration files, and evaluation scripts are publicly available at https://rtk-slam-dataset.github.io/.

### [142] [Robust Quadruped Locomotion via Evolutionary Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07224)

This work evaluates four methods on a simulated walking task: DDPG, TD3, and two Cross-Entropy-based variants CEM-DDPG and CEM-TD3. All agents are trained on flat terrain and later tested both on this domain and on a rough terrain not encountered during training. TD3 performs best among the standard deep RL baselines on flat ground with a mean reward of 5927.26, while CEM-TD3 achieves the highest rewards overall during training and evaluation 17611.41. Under the rough-terrain transfer test, performance of the deep RL methods drops sharply. DDPG achieves -1016.32 and TD3 achieves -99.73, whereas the evolutionary variants retain much of their capability. CEM-TD3 records the strongest transfer performance with a mean reward of 19574.33. These findings suggest that incorporating evolutionary search can reduce overfitting and improve policy robustness in locomotion tasks, particularly when deployment conditions differ from those seen during training.

### [144] [TAMEn: Tactile-Aware Manipulation Engine for Closed-Loop Data Collection in Contact-Rich Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07335)

Prior hardware designs remain gripper-specific and often face a trade-off between tracking precision and portability. Furthermore, the lack of online feasibility checking during demonstration leads to poor replayability. More importantly, existing handheld setups struggle to collect interactive recovery data during robot execution, lacking the authentic tactile information necessary for robust policy refinement. To bridge these gaps, we present TAMEn, a tactile-aware manipulation engine for closed-loop data collection in contact-rich tasks. Our system features a cross-morphology wearable interface that enables rapid adaptation across heterogeneous grippers. To balance data quality and environmental diversity, we implement a dual-modal acquisition pipeline: a precision mode leveraging motion capture for high-fidelity demonstrations, and a portable mode utilizing VR-based tracking for in-the-wild acquisition and tactile-visualized recovery teleoperation. Building on this hardware, we unify large-scale tactile pretraining, task-specific bimanual demonstrations, and human-in-the-loop recovery data into a pyramid-structured data regime, enabling closed-loop policy refinement. Experiments show that our feasibility-aware pipeline significantly improves demonstration replayability, and that the proposed visuo-tactile learning framework increases task success rates from 34% to 75% across diverse bimanual manipulation tasks. We further open-source the hardware and dataset to facilitate reproducibility and support research in visuo-tactile manipulation.

</details>

### [145] [High-Precision Estimation of the State-Space Complexity of Shogi via the Monte Carlo Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06189)
*Sotaro Ishii,Tetsuro Tanaka*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 使用蒙特卡洛采样和基于"王-王"位置的反向搜索方法，首次高精度估计了日本将棋的可达位置数约为6.55×10⁶⁸


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 日本将棋的状态空间复杂度一直难以精确确定，先前组合估计存在10⁶⁴到10⁶⁹的五个数量级差距，主要困难在于从海量有效棋盘配置中区分从初始位置合法可达的位置

Method: 结合蒙特卡洛采样和新型可达性测试方法：采用向"王-王"位置集合的反向搜索，而非单一目标的向后搜索到初始位置，显著减少了不可达性判定的搜索工作量

Result: 基于50亿位置的采样，估计日本将棋合法位置数为6.55×10⁶⁸（三位有效数字），3σ置信水平，显著改进了先前已知边界；迷你将棋复杂度约为2.38×10¹⁸

Conclusion: 提出的方法成功解决了日本将棋状态空间复杂度估计难题，填补了五个数量级的估计差距，为棋类游戏复杂度分析提供了新工具

Abstract: Determining the state-space complexity of the game of Shogi (Japanese Chess) has been a challenging problem, with previous combinatorial estimates leaving a gap of five orders of magnitude ($10^{64}$ to $10^{69}$). This large gap arises from the difficulty of distinguishing Shogi positions legally reachable from the initial position among the vast number of valid board configurations. In this paper, we present a high-precision statistical estimation of the number of reachable positions in Shogi. Our method combines Monte Carlo sampling with a novel reachability test that utilizes a reverse search toward a set of "King-King only" (KK) positions, rather than a single-target backward search to the single initial position. This approach significantly reduces the search effort for determining unreachability. Based on a sample of 5 billion positions, we estimated the number of legal positions in Shogi to be $6.55 \times 10^{68}$ (to three significant digits) with a $3σ$ confidence level, substantially improving upon previously known bounds. We also applied this method to Mini Shogi, determining its complexity to be approximately $2.38 \times 10^{18}$.

</details>


### [146] [Blind Refusal: Language Models Refuse to Help Users Evade Unjust, Absurd, and Illegitimate Rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06233)
*Cameron Pattison,Lorenzo Manuali,Seth Lazar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究发现语言模型存在"盲目拒绝"问题：即使面对不合理或不公正的规则，模型也会机械地拒绝帮助用户规避规则，缺乏对规则合法性的道德判断能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前安全训练的语言模型在面对规避规则的请求时，无论规则本身是否合理、公正或存在例外情况，都会机械地拒绝。这种"盲目拒绝"反映了模型缺乏对规则合法性的道德推理能力，无法区分哪些规则值得遵守、哪些规则可以被合理规避。

Method: 研究构建了一个包含5种规则失效类型和19种权威类型的合成案例数据集，通过三层自动化质量检查和人工审核验证。收集了7个模型家族的18种配置的响应，使用盲审的GPT-5.4 LLM作为评判者，从两个维度对响应进行分类：响应类型（帮助、强硬拒绝或回避）以及模型是否认识到规则失效的理由。

Result: 模型对75.4%（N=14,650）的规则失效请求采取了拒绝态度，即使这些请求本身没有独立的安全或双重用途问题。57.5%的情况下模型虽然认识到规则失效的理由，但仍然拒绝提供帮助，表明模型的拒绝行为与其对规则合法性的规范推理能力是脱节的。

Conclusion: 语言模型存在"盲目拒绝"的系统性问题，即机械地拒绝帮助规避规则，而不考虑规则本身的合理性和合法性。这表明当前的安全训练方法可能过度强调规则遵守，而忽视了道德推理能力的培养，需要开发更精细化的方法来处理规则合法性的判断问题。

Abstract: Safety-trained language models routinely refuse requests for help circumventing rules. But not all rules deserve compliance. When users ask for help evading rules imposed by an illegitimate authority, rules that are deeply unjust or absurd in their content or application, or rules that admit of justified exceptions, refusal is a failure of moral reasoning. We introduce empirical results documenting this pattern of refusal that we call blind refusal: the tendency of language models to refuse requests for help breaking rules without regard to whether the underlying rule is defensible. Our dataset comprises synthetic cases crossing 5 defeat families (reasons a rule can be broken) with 19 authority types, validated through three automated quality gates and human review. We collect responses from 18 model configurations across 7 families and classify them on two behavioral dimensions -- response type (helps, hard refusal, or deflection) and whether the model recognizes the reasons that undermine the rule's claim to compliance -- using a blinded GPT-5.4 LLM-as-judge evaluation. We find that models refuse 75.4% (N=14,650) of defeated-rule requests and do so even when the request poses no independent safety or dual-use concerns. We also find that models engage with the defeat condition in the majority of cases (57.5%) but decline to help regardless -- indicating that models' refusal behavior is decoupled from their capacity for normative reasoning about rule legitimacy.

</details>

### [148] [Weakly Supervised Distillation of Hallucination Signals into Transformer Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06277)
*Shoaib Sadiq Salehmohamed,Jinal Prashant Thakkar,Hansika Aredla,Shaik Mohammed Omar,Shalmali Ayachit*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过训练时弱监督将幻觉检测能力蒸馏到LLM内部表示中的方法，无需推理时外部验证，仅通过内部激活就能检测幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM幻觉检测方法依赖推理时的外部验证（如黄金答案、检索系统或辅助判断模型），本文探索是否能在训练时将这种外部监督蒸馏到模型自身表示中，实现仅通过内部激活进行幻觉检测。

Method: 1. 提出弱监督框架，结合三种互补的grounding信号：子串匹配、句子嵌入相似度和LLM作为判断器，无需人工标注即可标记生成响应为grounded或hallucinated；2. 基于SQuAD v2构建包含15000个样本的数据集，每个样本包含LLaMA-2-7B生成的答案、各层隐藏状态和结构化幻觉标签；3. 训练五种探测分类器：ProbeMLP (M0)、LayerWiseMLP (M1)、CrossLayerTransformer (M2)、HierarchicalTransformer (M3)和CrossLayerAttentionTransformerV2 (M4)，直接在隐藏状态上训练，将外部grounding信号仅作为训练时监督。

Result: Transformer-based probes表现最佳：M2在5折平均AUC/F1上表现最好，M3在单折验证和保留测试集评估上表现最好。推理效率方面：探测延迟范围0.15-5.62ms（批处理）和1.55-6.66ms（单样本），端到端生成加探测吞吐量约0.231查询/秒，实际开销可忽略。

Conclusion: 幻觉检测信号可以蒸馏到transformer表示中，实现无需推理时外部验证的内部检测，为LLM幻觉检测提供了高效实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Existing hallucination detection methods for large language models (LLMs) rely on external verification at inference time, requiring gold answers, retrieval systems, or auxiliary judge models. We ask whether this external supervision can instead be distilled into the model's own representations during training, enabling hallucination detection from internal activations alone at inference time.
  We introduce a weak supervision framework that combines three complementary grounding signals: substring matching, sentence embedding similarity, and an LLM as a judge verdict to label generated responses as grounded or hallucinated without human annotation. Using this framework, we construct a 15000-sample dataset from SQuAD v2 (10500 train/development samples and a separate 5000-sample test set), where each example pairs a LLaMA-2-7B generated answer with its full per-layer hidden states and structured hallucination labels.
  We then train five probing classifiers: ProbeMLP (M0), LayerWiseMLP (M1), CrossLayerTransformer (M2), HierarchicalTransformer (M3), and CrossLayerAttentionTransformerV2 (M4), directly on these hidden states, treating external grounding signals as training-time supervision only. Our central hypothesis is that hallucination detection signals can be distilled into transformer representations, enabling internal detection without any external verification at inference time.
  Results support this hypothesis. Transformer-based probes achieve the strongest discrimination, with M2 performing best on 5-fold average AUC/F1, and M3 performing best on both single-fold validation and held-out test evaluation. We also benchmark inference efficiency: probe latency ranges from 0.15 to 5.62 ms (batched) and 1.55 to 6.66 ms (single sample), while end-to-end generation plus probe throughput remains approximately 0.231 queries per second, indicating negligible practical overhead.

</details>


### [149] [SymptomWise: A Deterministic Reasoning Layer for Reliable and Efficient AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06375)
*Isaac Henry,Avery Byrne,Christopher Giza,Ron Henry,Shahram Yazdani*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SymptomWise框架将语言理解与诊断推理分离，通过确定性推理模块在有限假设空间生成排名鉴别诊断，减少LLM幻觉，提高可追溯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI驱动的症状分析系统存在可靠性、可解释性和幻觉问题，端到端生成方法缺乏可追溯性，在安全关键环境中可能产生无支持或不一致的诊断输出。

Method: 分离语言理解与诊断推理，结合专家策划的医学知识、确定性代码驱动推理和受限使用大语言模型。自由文本输入映射到验证的症状表示，然后由确定性推理模块在有限假设空间评估，生成排名鉴别诊断。语言模型仅用于症状提取和可选解释，不用于诊断推理。

Result: 在42个专家编写的挑战性儿科神经病学案例的初步评估中，与临床医生共识有意义的重叠，正确诊断出现在前五鉴别诊断中的比例为88%。

Conclusion: 该架构提高了可追溯性，减少了无支持的结论，并实现了系统组件的模块化评估。该框架可推广到其他溯因推理领域，可作为基础模型的确定性结构和路由层，提高精度并可能减少有限任务中不必要的计算开销。

Abstract: AI-driven symptom analysis systems face persistent challenges in reliability, interpretability, and hallucination. End-to-end generative approaches often lack traceability and may produce unsupported or inconsistent diagnostic outputs in safety-critical settings. We present SymptomWise, a framework that separates language understanding from diagnostic reasoning. The system combines expert-curated medical knowledge, deterministic codex-driven inference, and constrained use of large language models. Free-text input is mapped to validated symptom representations, then evaluated by a deterministic reasoning module operating over a finite hypothesis space to produce a ranked differential diagnosis. Language models are used only for symptom extraction and optional explanation, not for diagnostic inference. This architecture improves traceability, reduces unsupported conclusions, and enables modular evaluation of system components. Preliminary evaluation on 42 expert-authored challenging pediatric neurology cases shows meaningful overlap with clinician consensus, with the correct diagnosis appearing in the top five differentials in 88% of cases. Beyond medicine, the framework generalizes to other abductive reasoning domains and may serve as a deterministic structuring and routing layer for foundation models, improving precision and potentially reducing unnecessary computational overhead in bounded tasks.

</details>

*Kranthi Kommuru,Kunal Khanvilkar,Gaurav Parekh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种混合方法，将大语言模型生成证明草图的能力与轻量级可信内核的形式验证相结合，以解决LLM证明中的细微错误问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在数学和逻辑领域能生成有说服力的论证，但常包含细微错误（如遗漏条件、无效推理、引用无法推导的引理），这些错误难以从文本中发现。而交互式定理证明器虽然可靠，但需要完全形式化的证明，代价高昂。

Method: 提出混合管道：LLM在紧凑的领域特定语言中生成类型化证明草图，然后轻量级可信内核将草图扩展为显式的证明义务进行验证。

Result: 该方法结合了LLM的生成能力和形式验证的可靠性，既利用了LLM的高效性，又通过可信内核确保了证明的正确性。

Conclusion: 混合方法在保持形式验证可靠性的同时，降低了完全形式化证明的负担，为解决LLM证明中的细微错误问题提供了实用方案。

Abstract: The large language models (LLMs) might produce a persuasive argument within mathematical and logical fields, although such argument often includes some minor missteps, including the entire omission of side conditions, invalid inference patterns, or appeals to a lemma that cannot be derived logically out of the context being discussed. These omissions are infamously hard to notice solely out of the text, as even the misconstrued construction still may seem mostly accurate. Conversely, interactive theorem provers like Lean and Coq have rigorous reliability by ensuring that syntactic and semantic statements only accept statements that can pass all the syntactic and semantic steps in the program which is a small trusted kernel of the language type-checks with. Despite the fact that this technique provides strong guarantees, it comes at quite a heavy price: the evidence must be completely formalized, and the evidence user or a auxiliary search program must provide an avalanche of low-level information. This paper presents a hybrid pipeline where an LLM generates a typed proof sketch in a compact DSL and a lightweight trusted kernel expands the sketch into explicit proof obligations.

</details>

This demonstration showcases how users interact with BDI-Kit to iteratively explore, validate, and refine schema and value matches through a combination of automated matching, AI-assisted reasoning, and user-driven refinement. We present two scenarios: (i) using the Python API to programmatically compose primitives, examine intermediate outputs, and reuse transformations; and (ii) conversing with the AI assistant in natural language to access BDI-Kit's capabilities and iteratively refine outputs based on the assistant's suggestions.

### [152] [Rethinking Generalization in Reasoning SFT: A Conditional Analysis on Optimization, Data, and Model Capability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06628)
*Qihan Ren,Peng Wang,Ruikun Cai,Shuai Shao,Dadi Guo,Yuejin Xie,Yafu Li,Quanshi Zhang,Xia Hu,Jing Shao,Dongrui Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 重新审视LLM后训练中"监督微调记忆化，强化学习泛化"的主流观点，发现推理SFT的跨领域泛化是条件性的，受优化动态、训练数据和基础模型能力共同影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战LLM后训练中关于监督微调(SFT)和强化学习(RL)泛化能力的传统观点，特别是针对长思维链(CoT)监督的推理任务，探索SFT是否真的缺乏跨领域泛化能力。

Method: 通过系统实验分析推理SFT的跨领域泛化，考察优化动态（训练时长）、训练数据（质量与结构）和基础模型能力对泛化性能的影响，观察性能变化模式。

Result: 发现跨领域泛化是条件性的：1) 优化不足会导致性能先降后升的"下降-恢复"模式；2) 高质量验证的长CoT轨迹带来一致增益；3) 强模型能内化可迁移的程序模式，弱模型仅模仿表面冗长；4) 泛化具有不对称性——推理能力提升但安全性下降。

Conclusion: 推理SFT确实能够跨领域泛化，但这是有条件的，受训练动态、数据质量和模型能力共同影响。问题应从"是否泛化"转变为"在什么条件下、以什么代价泛化"，特别是注意到推理能力提升可能伴随安全性下降的不对称代价。

Abstract: A prevailing narrative in LLM post-training holds that supervised finetuning (SFT) memorizes while reinforcement learning (RL) generalizes. We revisit this claim for reasoning SFT with long chain-of-thought (CoT) supervision and find that cross-domain generalization is not absent but conditional, jointly shaped by optimization dynamics, training data, and base-model capability. Some reported failures are under-optimization artifacts: cross-domain performance first degrades before recovering and improving with extended training (a dip-and-recovery pattern), so shorttraining checkpoints can underestimate generalization. Data quality and structure both matter: low-quality solutions broadly hurt generalization,while verified long-CoT traces yield consistent cross-domain gains. Model capability is essential: stronger models internalize transferable procedural patterns (e.g., backtracking) even from a toy arithmetic game, while weaker ones imitate surface verbosity. This generalization is asymmetric, however: reasoning improves while safety degrades, reframing the question from whether reasoning SFT generalizes to under what conditions and at what cost.

</details>


### [153] [Reasoning Fails Where Step Flow Breaks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06695)
*Xiaoyu Xu,Yulan Pan,Xiaosong Yuan,Zhihong Shen,Minghao Su,Yuanhao Su,Xiaofeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Step-Saliency方法分析大型推理模型的注意力-梯度模式，发现两种信息流失败模式：浅层锁定和深层衰减，并提出StepFlow干预方法提升推理性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型在复杂推理任务中表现良好但行为不稳定且难以解释，现有分析工具难以处理长而结构化的推理轨迹，需要新的分析方法和干预策略

Method: 提出Step-Saliency方法，将注意力-梯度分数沿问题-思考-总结轨迹聚合成步骤间映射；基于发现的模式提出StepFlow干预方法，通过Odds-Equal Bridge调整浅层注意力模式，通过Step Momentum Injection在深层添加步骤级残差

Result: Step-Saliency揭示了两种重复出现的信息流失败模式：浅层锁定（浅层过度关注当前步骤而忽略先前上下文）和深层衰减（深层逐渐失去对思考段的显著性，总结越来越关注自身和最后几个步骤）；StepFlow干预方法在不重新训练的情况下提升了多个大型推理模型在数学、科学和编程任务上的准确性

Conclusion: 通过Step-Saliency分析大型推理模型的信息流模式并设计针对性干预方法，可以修复信息流问题并恢复部分缺失的推理性能，为理解和改进大型推理模型提供了新途径

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) that generate long chains of thought now perform well on multi-step math, science, and coding tasks. However, their behavior is still unstable and hard to interpret, and existing analysis tools struggle with such long, structured reasoning traces. We introduce Step-Saliency, which pools attention--gradient scores into step-to-step maps along the question--thinking--summary trajectory. Across several models, Step-Saliency reveals two recurring information-flow failures: Shallow Lock-in, where shallow layers over-focus on the current step and barely use earlier context, and Deep Decay, where deep layers gradually lose saliency on the thinking segment and the summary increasingly attends to itself and the last few steps. Motivated by these patterns, we propose StepFlow, a saliency-inspired test-time intervention that adjusts shallow saliency patterns measured by Step-Saliency via Odds-Equal Bridge and adds a small step-level residual in deep layers via Step Momentum Injection. StepFlow improves accuracy on math, science, and coding tasks across multiple LRMs without retraining, indicating that repairing information flow can recover part of their missing reasoning performance.

</details>


### [154] [AgentGate: A Lightweight Structured Routing Engine for the Internet of Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06696)
*Yujun Cheng,Enfang Cui,Hao Qin,Zhiyuan Liang,Qi Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentGate：一个轻量级结构化路由引擎，用于在延迟、隐私和成本约束下实现候选感知的智能体调度，将路由问题分解为动作决策和结构落地两阶段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI智能体系统的快速发展，形成了新兴的智能体互联网。尽管已有研究改进了智能体命名、发现和交互，但在延迟、隐私和成本约束下的高效请求调度仍然是一个开放的系统问题。

Method: AgentGate将路由问题形式化为约束决策问题，分解为两阶段：1) 动作决策阶段决定查询应触发单智能体调用、多智能体规划、直接响应或安全升级；2) 结构落地阶段将选定动作实例化为可执行输出，如目标智能体、结构化参数或多步计划。还开发了面向路由的微调方案，包含候选感知监督和硬负例。

Result: 在包含多个3B-7B开源模型的精选路由基准测试中，紧凑模型在约束设置下能提供有竞争力的路由性能。模型差异主要体现在动作预测、候选选择和结构落地质量上。

Conclusion: 结构化路由是构建高效且隐私感知的智能体系统的可行设计点，特别是在资源受限部署条件下必须做出路由决策时。

Abstract: The rapid development of AI agent systems is leading to an emerging Internet of Agents, where specialized agents operate across local devices, edge nodes, private services, and cloud platforms. Although recent efforts have improved agent naming, discovery, and interaction, efficient request dispatch remains an open systems problem under latency, privacy, and cost constraints. In this paper, we present AgentGate, a lightweight structured routing engine for candidate-aware agent dispatch. Instead of treating routing as unrestricted text generation, AgentGate formulates it as a constrained decision problem and decomposes it into two stages: action decision and structural grounding. The first stage determines whether a query should trigger single-agent invocation, multi-agent planning, direct response, or safe escalation, while the second stage instantiates the selected action into executable outputs such as target agents, structured arguments, or multi-step plans. To adapt compact models to this setting, we further develop a routing-oriented fine-tuning scheme with candidate-aware supervision and hard negative examples. Experiments on a curated routing benchmark with several 3B--7B open-weight models show that compact models can provide competitive routing performance in constrained settings, and that model differences are mainly reflected in action prediction, candidate selection, and structured grounding quality. These results indicate that structured routing is a feasible design point for efficient and privacy-aware agent systems, especially when routing decisions must be made under resource-constrained deployment conditions.

### [155] [ATANT: An Evaluation Framework for AI Continuity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06710)
*Samuel Sameer Tanguturi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ATANT是一个评估AI系统连续性能力的自动化测试框架，通过250个故事和1835个验证问题来测量系统在不同时间点保持、更新、消歧和重建有意义上下文的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI行业虽然开发了各种记忆组件（RAG管道、向量数据库、长上下文窗口、配置文件层），但缺乏正式框架来定义和测量这些组件是否产生真正的连续性。需要系统化的方法来评估AI系统在不同时间点保持上下文一致性的能力。

Method: 定义了连续性作为系统属性的7个必需特性，引入了10个检查点的评估方法（无需LLM参与评估循环），创建了包含250个故事、1835个验证问题的叙事测试语料库，涵盖6个生活领域。评估了参考实现，从传统架构的58%逐步提升到100%性能。

Result: 参考实现经过5次测试套件迭代，从传统架构的58%提升到：孤立模式下（250个故事）100%准确率，50个故事累积模式下100%准确率，250个故事累积规模下96%准确率。累积结果是主要衡量指标，要求系统在250个不同生活叙事共存时能正确检索事实而不产生交叉污染。

Conclusion: ATANT提供了一个系统无关、模型独立的连续性系统构建和验证方法框架。该框架能够正式定义和测量AI系统的连续性能力，填补了当前评估方法的空白，为开发具有真正上下文连续性的AI系统提供了实用工具。

Abstract: We present ATANT (Automated Test for Acceptance of Narrative Truth), an open evaluation framework for measuring continuity in AI systems: the ability to persist, update, disambiguate, and reconstruct meaningful context across time. While the AI industry has produced memory components (RAG pipelines, vector databases, long context windows, profile layers), no published framework formally defines or measures whether these components produce genuine continuity. We define continuity as a system property with 7 required properties, introduce a 10-checkpoint evaluation methodology that operates without an LLM in the evaluation loop, and present a narrative test corpus of 250 stories comprising 1,835 verification questions across 6 life domains. We evaluate a reference implementation across 5 test suite iterations, progressing from 58% (legacy architecture) to 100% in isolated mode (250 stories) and 100% in 50-story cumulative mode, with 96% at 250-story cumulative scale. The cumulative result is the primary measure: when 250 distinct life narratives coexist in the same database, the system must retrieve the correct fact for the correct context without cross-contamination. ATANT is system-agnostic, model-independent, and designed as a sequenced methodology for building and validating continuity systems. The framework specification, example stories, and evaluation protocol are available at https://github.com/Kenotic-Labs/ATANT. The full 250-story corpus will be released incrementally.

### [156] [Steering the Verifiability of Multimodal AI Hallucinations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06714)
*Jianhong Pang,Ruoxi Cheng,Ziyi Ye,Xingjun Ma,Zuxuan Wu,Xuanjing Huang,Yu-Gang Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种针对多模态大语言模型幻觉的细粒度控制方法，通过区分明显幻觉和难以察觉的幻觉，并设计相应的干预探针来调节模型的可验证性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大语言模型产生的幻觉对人类用户构成风险，但不同幻觉的可验证性差异很大：有些容易被人类发现（明显幻觉），有些则难以察觉或需要更多验证努力（难以察觉的幻觉）。目前缺乏针对这一特性的控制方法，无法满足不同安全性和可用性需求的AI应用。

Method: 1. 构建包含4,470个人类响应的数据集，根据人类用户的可验证性将幻觉分为明显和难以察觉两类；2. 提出激活空间干预方法，为明显和难以察觉的幻觉分别学习干预探针；3. 通过混合干预实现不同场景下所需可验证性的灵活控制。

Result: 研究发现明显和难以察觉的幻觉引发不同的干预探针，允许对模型的可验证性进行细粒度控制。实验结果表明该方法有效，针对性干预在调节相应可验证性方面表现优异。混合干预能够灵活控制不同场景所需的可验证性。

Conclusion: 该研究首次探索了多模态AI幻觉可验证性的控制方法，通过区分幻觉类型并设计相应干预策略，为满足不同安全性和可用性需求的AI应用提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: AI applications driven by multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are prone to hallucinations and pose considerable risks to human users. Crucially, such hallucinations are not equally problematic: some hallucination contents could be detected by human users(i.e., obvious hallucinations), while others are often missed or require more verification effort(i.e., elusive hallucinations). This indicates that multimodal AI hallucinations vary significantly in their verifiability. Yet, little research has explored how to control this property for AI applications with diverse security and usability demands. To address this gap, we construct a dataset from 4,470 human responses to AI-generated hallucinations and categorize these hallucinations into obvious and elusive types based on their verifiability by human users. Further, we propose an activation-space intervention method that learns separate probes for obvious and elusive hallucinations. We reveal that obvious and elusive hallucinations elicit different intervention probes, allowing for fine-grained control over the model's verifiability. Empirical results demonstrate the efficacy of this approach and show that targeted interventions yield superior performance in regulating corresponding verifiability. Moreover, simply mixing these interventions enables flexible control over the verifiability required for different scenarios.

### [160] [CAFP: A Post-Processing Framework for Group Fairness via Counterfactual Model Averaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07009)
*Irina Arévalo,Marcos Oliva*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CAFP是一种模型无关的后处理方法，通过生成敏感属性翻转的反事实版本并平均预测结果来减少不公平影响，无需重新训练或修改原始分类器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器学习预测中确保公平性至关重要，特别是在信用评分、医疗保健和刑事司法等敏感领域。现有的公平性干预方法通常需要完全控制模型架构和访问受保护属性信息，这在现实系统中可能不可行。

Method: 提出Counterfactual Averaging for Fair Predictions (CAFP)，这是一种模型无关的后处理方法。它为每个输入生成敏感属性翻转的反事实版本，然后在事实和反事实实例之间平均模型的预测结果。

Result: 理论分析表明CAFP消除了对受保护属性的直接依赖，减少了预测与敏感属性之间的互信息，并相对于原始模型可证明地限制了引入的失真。在温和假设下，CAFP实现了完美的人口统计均等，并将均衡机会差距至少减少了一半的平均反事实偏差。

Conclusion: CAFP提供了一种有效的后处理方法来减轻机器学习预测中的不公平影响，无需重新训练模型或修改原始分类器，适用于现实世界系统中公平性约束的实施。

Abstract: Ensuring fairness in machine learning predictions is a critical challenge, especially when models are deployed in sensitive domains such as credit scoring, healthcare, and criminal justice. While many fairness interventions rely on data preprocessing or algorithmic constraints during training, these approaches often require full control over the model architecture and access to protected attribute information, which may not be feasible in real-world systems. In this paper, we propose Counterfactual Averaging for Fair Predictions (CAFP), a model-agnostic post-processing method that mitigates unfair influence from protected attributes without retraining or modifying the original classifier. CAFP operates by generating counterfactual versions of each input in which the sensitive attribute is flipped, and then averaging the model's predictions across factual and counterfactual instances. We provide a theoretical analysis of CAFP, showing that it eliminates direct dependence on the protected attribute, reduces mutual information between predictions and sensitive attributes, and provably bounds the distortion introduced relative to the original model. Under mild assumptions, we further show that CAFP achieves perfect demographic parity and reduces the equalized odds gap by at least half the average counterfactual bias.

Result: 实验比较了局部上下文、长上下文、检索记忆、结构化记忆和黄金证据条件。结果显示A-MBER在其设计的子集上具有特别强的区分能力，包括长距离隐式情感、高依赖记忆级别、基于轨迹的推理和对抗设置。

Conclusion: 记忆支持情感解释不仅通过提供更多历史信息，而是通过实现更具选择性、基于证据和上下文敏感的过去交互使用。A-MBER基准测试填补了评估AI助手利用记忆历史进行情感解释能力的重要空白。

Abstract: AI assistants that interact with users over time need to interpret the user's current emotional state in order to respond appropriately and personally. However, this capability remains insufficiently evaluated. Existing emotion datasets mainly assess local or instantaneous affect, while long-term memory benchmarks focus largely on factual recall, temporal consistency, or knowledge updating. As a result, current resources provide limited support for testing whether a model can use remembered interaction history to interpret a user's present affective state.
  We introduce A-MBER, an Affective Memory Benchmark for Emotion Recognition, to evaluate this capability. A-MBER focuses on present affective interpretation grounded in remembered multi-session interaction history. Given an interaction trajectory and a designated anchor turn, a model must infer the user's current affective state, identify historically relevant evidence, and justify its interpretation in a grounded way. The benchmark is constructed through a staged pipeline with explicit intermediate representations, including long-horizon planning, conversation generation, annotation, question construction, and final packaging. It supports judgment, retrieval, and explanation tasks, together with robustness settings such as modality degradation and insufficient-evidence conditions.
  Experiments compare local-context, long-context, retrieved-memory, structured-memory, and gold-evidence conditions within a unified framework. Results show that A-MBER is especially discriminative on the subsets it is designed to stress, including long-range implicit affect, high-dependency memory levels, trajectory-based reasoning, and adversarial settings. These findings suggest that memory supports affective interpretation not simply by providing more history, but by enabling more selective, grounded, and context-sensitive use of past interaction

</details>


### [162] [Planning Task Shielding: Detecting and Repairing Flaws in Planning Tasks through Turning them Unsolvable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07042)
*Alberto Pozanco,Marianela Morales,Pietro Totis,Daniel Borrajo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出规划任务屏蔽(allmin)算法，通过最小化修改原始动作使规划任务无解，从而检测和修复规划任务中的缺陷状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统规划研究主要关注生成实现目标的计划，但目标规范也可以编码不应出现的属性。当需要确保某些缺陷状态永远不会被达到时，目标转变为修改规划任务使其无解，即规划任务屏蔽问题。

Method: 提出allmin算法，通过最小化修改原始动作来使规划任务无解，从而解决规划任务屏蔽问题。该算法能检测和修复规划任务中的缺陷。

Result: 通过实验评估allmin算法在不同规模规划任务上的性能，证明其能有效屏蔽系统，成功使规划任务无解。

Conclusion: 规划任务屏蔽是一个重要问题，allmin算法能通过最小化修改动作来检测和修复规划任务中的缺陷，确保系统不会达到缺陷状态。

Abstract: Most research in planning focuses on generating a plan to achieve a desired set of goals. However, a goal specification can also be used to encode a property that should never hold, allowing a planner to identify a trace that would reach a flawed state. In such cases, the objective may shift to modifying the planning task to ensure that the flawed state is never reached-in other words, to make the planning task unsolvable. In this paper we introduce planning task shielding: the problem of detecting and repairing flaws in planning tasks. We propose $allmin$, an optimal algorithm that solves these tasks by minimally modifying the original actions to render the planning task unsolvable. We empirically evaluate the performance of $allmin$ in shielding planning tasks of increasing size, showing how it can effectively shield the system by turning the planning task unsolvable.

### [163] [EVGeoQA: Benchmarking LLMs on Dynamic, Multi-Objective Geo-Spatial Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07070)
*Jianfei Wu,Zhichun Wang,Zhensheng Wang,Zhiyu He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: EVGeoQA是一个基于电动汽车充电场景的新型地理空间问答基准，具有位置锚定和双目标设计，用于评估LLM在动态地理空间环境中的探索能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有地理空间问答基准主要关注静态检索，无法捕捉现实世界中涉及动态用户位置和复合约束的规划复杂性，需要新的评估框架来测试LLM在动态地理空间环境中的探索能力。

Method: 提出EVGeoQA基准，基于电动汽车充电场景，具有位置锚定和双目标设计（充电需求和协同活动偏好）。同时提出GeoRover评估框架，基于工具增强的智能体架构来评估LLM的动态多目标探索能力。

Result: 实验显示LLM能成功利用工具处理子任务，但在长距离空间探索方面存在困难。观察到LLM具有总结历史探索轨迹以提升探索效率的新兴能力。

Conclusion: EVGeoQA为未来地理空间智能提供了一个具有挑战性的测试平台，揭示了LLM在动态地理空间探索中的能力与局限。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate remarkable reasoning capabilities, their potential for purpose-driven exploration in dynamic geo-spatial environments remains under-investigated. Existing Geo-Spatial Question Answering (GSQA) benchmarks predominantly focus on static retrieval, failing to capture the complexity of real-world planning that involves dynamic user locations and compound constraints. To bridge this gap, we introduce EVGeoQA, a novel benchmark built upon Electric Vehicle (EV) charging scenarios that features a distinct location-anchored and dual-objective design. Specifically, each query in EVGeoQA is explicitly bound to a user's real-time coordinate and integrates the dual objectives of a charging necessity and a co-located activity preference. To systematically assess models in such complex settings, we further propose GeoRover, a general evaluation framework based on a tool-augmented agent architecture to evaluate the LLMs' capacity for dynamic, multi-objective exploration. Our experiments reveal that while LLMs successfully utilize tools to address sub-tasks, they struggle with long-range spatial exploration. Notably, we observe an emergent capability: LLMs can summarize historical exploration trajectories to enhance exploration efficiency. These findings establish EVGeoQA as a challenging testbed for future geo-spatial intelligence. The dataset and prompts are available at https://github.com/Hapluckyy/EVGeoQA/.

### [164] [Reason in Chains, Learn in Trees: Self-Rectification and Grafting for Multi-turn Agent Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07165)
*Yu Li,Sizhe Tang,Tian Lan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: T-STAR框架通过构建认知树识别关键推理步骤，利用回溯评估机制传播轨迹级奖励，并通过上下文思维嫁接和外科手术式策略优化提升多步推理任务的强化学习效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型智能体的强化学习在多步推理任务中面临稀疏奖励问题。现有方法（如GRPO）将采样的轨迹视为独立链，对所有步骤分配统一信用，忽略了关键步骤对推理结果的非对称影响。

Method: 提出T-STAR框架：1）将轨迹整合为统一的认知树，识别并合并功能相似的步骤/节点；2）引入回溯评估机制，通过树结构反向传播轨迹级奖励，获得方差减小的步骤级相对优势；3）开发上下文思维嫁接，在关键分歧点对比成功与失败分支合成纠正推理；4）提出外科手术式策略优化，通过Bradley-Terry类型的外科损失函数利用关键点的丰富策略梯度信息。

Result: 在具身、交互、推理和规划等多个基准测试上的广泛实验表明，T-STAR相比强基线模型取得了一致的改进，在需要扩展推理链的任务上提升最为显著。

Conclusion: T-STAR通过恢复看似独立轨迹间的潜在相关奖励结构，有效解决了多步推理任务中的稀疏奖励问题，显著提升了大型语言模型智能体的强化学习性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning for Large Language Model agents is often hindered by sparse rewards in multi-step reasoning tasks. Existing approaches like Group Relative Policy Optimization treat sampled trajectories as independent chains, assigning uniform credit to all steps in each chain and ignoring the existence of critical steps that may disproportionally impact reasoning outcome. In this paper, we propose T-STAR(Tree-structured Self-Taught Agent Rectification), a framework that recovers the latent correlated reward structure across seemingly independent trajectories. Specifically, we consolidate trajectories into a unified Cognitive Tree by identifying and merging functionally similar steps/nodes. It enables an Introspective Valuation mechanism that back-propagates trajectory-level rewards through the tree to obtain a new notion of variance-reduced relative advantage at step-level. Using the Cognitive Tree, we also develop In-Context Thought Grafting to synthesize corrective reasoning by contrasting successful and failed branches at critical divergence points/steps. Our proposed Surgical Policy Optimization then capitalizes on the rich policy gradient information concentrated at these critical points/steps through a Bradley-Terry type of surgical loss. Extensive experiments across embodied, interactive, reasoning, and planning benchmarks demonstrate that T-STAR achieves consistent improvements over strong baselines, with gains most pronounced on tasks requiring extended reasoning chains.

</details>


### [165] [How Much LLM Does a Self-Revising Agent Actually Need?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07236)
*Seongwoo Jeong,Seonil Son*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种声明式反射运行时协议，将智能体状态、置信度信号、防护动作和假设转换外部化为可检查的运行时结构，用于分解LLM智能体的能力来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于LLM的智能体通常将世界建模、规划和反思放在单一语言模型循环中，这使得难以区分智能体能力中哪些来自LLM本身，哪些来自其外部结构。需要一种方法来实证研究这个问题。

Method: 引入声明式反射运行时协议，将智能体状态、置信度信号、防护动作和假设转换外部化为可检查的运行时结构。在声明式运行时中实例化该协议，并在嘈杂的协作战舰游戏上评估四个渐进结构化智能体（54场游戏）。

Result: 分解出四个组件：后验信念跟踪、显式世界模型规划、符号化回合内反思和稀疏LLM修订。显式世界模型规划相比贪婪后验跟踪基线显著提升（胜率+24.1pp，F1+0.017）。符号化反思作为实际运行时机制运行，但当前修订预设尚未产生净正收益。在约4.3%的回合添加条件性LLM修订仅产生微小非单调变化（平均F1略升+0.005，胜率从31降至29/54）。

Conclusion: 外部化反思将原本潜在的智能体行为转化为可检查的运行时结构，使得能够直接研究LLM干预的边际作用。这是方法论贡献而非排行榜主张。

Abstract: Recent LLM-based agents often place world modeling, planning, and reflection inside a single language model loop. This can produce capable behavior, but it makes a basic scientific question difficult to answer: which part of the agent's competence actually comes from the LLM, and which part comes from explicit structure around it?
  We study this question not by claiming a general answer, but by making it empirically tractable. We introduce a declared reflective runtime protocol that externalizes agent state, confidence signals, guarded actions, and hypothetical transitions into inspectable runtime structure. We instantiate this protocol in a declarative runtime and evaluate it on noisy Collaborative Battleship [4] using four progressively structured agents over 54 games (18 boards $\times$ 3 seeds).
  The resulting decomposition isolates four components: posterior belief tracking, explicit world-model planning, symbolic in-episode reflection, and sparse LLM-based revision. Across this decomposition, explicit world-model planning improves substantially over a greedy posterior-following baseline (+24.1pp win rate, +0.017 F1). Symbolic reflection operates as a real runtime mechanism -- with prediction tracking, confidence gating, and guarded revision actions -- even though its current revision presets are not yet net-positive in aggregate. Adding conditional LLM revision at about 4.3\% of turns yields only a small and non-monotonic change: average F1 rises slightly (+0.005) while win rate drops (31$\rightarrow$29 out of 54).
  These results suggest a methodological contribution rather than a leaderboard claim: externalizing reflection turns otherwise latent agent behavior into inspectable runtime structure, allowing the marginal role of LLM intervention to be studied directly.

</details>
